giga_megaview_vat_01 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {}
}

# Ether Drake
giga_vat_01_grow_01_started = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_01
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_01_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_01
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_01_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_01_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_01_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_01_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_01_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_01
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_01_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_01_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_01_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_01_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_01_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_01_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_01_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_01
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_01
			clear_variable = the_vat_01_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_01_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_01_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_01 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_01_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_01_energy_cost }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_requires_leviathan_slain_dragon"
			from = { has_country_flag = giga_vat_can_clone_dragon }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_01
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_01
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_01_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_01_2_00_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.10001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_01_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_01_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_03_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_03
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_03_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_03_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_03_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_03_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_03_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_03
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_03_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_03_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_03_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_03_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_03_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_03_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_03_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_03
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_03
			clear_variable = the_vat_01_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_03_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_03_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_03 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_03_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_03_energy_cost }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_requires_leviathan_slain_tiyanki"
			from = { has_country_flag = giga_vat_can_clone_tiyanki }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_03
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_03
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_03_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_01_2_00_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.10001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_03_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_03_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_05_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_05
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_05_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_05_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_05_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_05_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_05_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_05
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_05_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_05_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_05_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_05_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_05_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_05_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_05_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_05
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_05
			clear_variable = the_vat_01_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_05_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_05_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_05 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_05_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_05_energy_cost }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_requires_leviathan_slain_voidspawn"
			from = { has_country_flag = giga_vat_can_clone_voidspawn }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_05
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_05
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_05_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_01_1_00_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.10001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_05_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_05_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_07
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_01_grow_07_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_07_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_07_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_01_grow_07 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_1
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_07
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_07
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_07_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_01_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.10001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_07_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_07_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_09
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_grow_09
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_01_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_01_grow_09_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_01_0_25_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.10001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_09_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_09_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_02_grow_06_started = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {}
}

giga_vat_02_grow_06_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_02_grow_06_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_02_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_02_grow_06_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_02_grow_06_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_02_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_02_grow_06_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_06
			clear_variable = the_vat_02_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_02_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_02_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_02_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_02_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.20001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_03_grow_06_started = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_06_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_03_grow_06_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_06_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_03_grow_06_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_06_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_06
			clear_variable = the_vat_03_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_03_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.30001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_07_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_07
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_03_grow_07_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_07_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_07_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_07_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_07
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_03_grow_07_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_07_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_07_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_07_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_07_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_07
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_07
			clear_variable = the_vat_03_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_07_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_07 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_07
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_07
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_07_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_03_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.30001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_07_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_07_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_09
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_03_grow_09_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_09_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_09_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_09_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {

		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_09

	effect = {

			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_09

		}
		from = {

		}
	}
}

giga_vat_03_grow_09 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_2
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_09
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_grow_09
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_03_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_03_grow_09_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_03_0_25_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.30001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_09_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_09_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_04_grow_06_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_04_grow_06_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_04_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_04_grow_06_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_04_grow_06_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_04_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_06
			clear_variable = the_vat_04_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_04_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_04_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_04_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_04_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.40001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_05_grow_06_started = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {}
}

giga_vat_05_grow_06_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_05_grow_06_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_05_grow_06_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_05_grow_06_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_05_grow_06_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06
			clear_variable = the_vat_05_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_05_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_05_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.50001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_07_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_05_grow_07 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		OR = {
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_3
			is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		}
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_07_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_07_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_07
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_grow_07
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_05_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_05_grow_07_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_05_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.50001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_07_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_07_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_06_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_06_grow_06_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_06_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_06_grow_06_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_06_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_06
			clear_variable = the_vat_06_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_06_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.60001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_09_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_09
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_06_grow_09_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_09_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_09_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_09_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_09_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_09
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_06_grow_09_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_09_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_09_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_09_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from

		}
		from = {

			add_resource = { energy = @grow_09_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_06_grow_09 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_09_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_09_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_09
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_grow_09
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_06_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_06_grow_09_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_06_0_25_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.60001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_09_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_09_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

# Swarm Queen
giga_vat_07_grow_06_started = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_06_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_07_grow_06_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_06_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_06
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_07_grow_06_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_06_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_06
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_06
			clear_variable = the_vat_07_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_06 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_06_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_06_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_06
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_06_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_07_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.70001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_06_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_06_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_08_minus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_08
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_07_grow_08_amount
				value > 1
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_08_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_08_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_08_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_08_plus = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_08
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = giga_vat_07_grow_08_amount
				value < 10
			}
			exists = from
		}
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_08_amount value = 1 }
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_08_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_08_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_08_cancel = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
		has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_08
	}
	allow = {}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = CANCEL
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
			remove_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_08
			clear_variable = the_vat_07_pixel
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_08_food_cost }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_08_energy_cost }
		}
	}
}

giga_vat_07_grow_08 = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = megastructure
		exists = from
		from = { is_same_value = prev.owner }
		is_megastructure_type = the_vat_4
		NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use }
	}
	allow = {
		hidden_trigger = { exists = from }
		from = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= @grow_08_food_cost }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @grow_08_energy_cost }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			custom_tooltip = giga_grow_08
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_grow_08
			set_megastructure_flag = giga_vat_07_in_use
			set_variable = { which = giga_vat_07_grow_08_amount value = 1 }
			planet = {
				set_timed_planet_flag = { flag = vat_07_0_50_day_pixel days = 5 }
				planet_event = { id = giga_progress_bars.70001 }
			}
		}
		from = {
			add_resource = { food = @grow_08_food_cost_deduct }
			add_resource = { energy = @grow_08_energy_cost_deduct }
		}
	}
}
